Heading level skipped: h1 to h4

<h4 class="tve-toggle-text" data-css="tve-u-1776c234bcd" style="">Styremøte</h4>
Don't skip heading levels. Use h2 instead of h4
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Page has no main landmark

<body>
Add <main> element or role='main' to wrap primary content

<a class="" href="https://sunnmoreregionrad.no/wp-content/uploads/2025/02/Referat-fra-styremote-nr.-1-2025-i-Sunnmore-regionrad-IKS-14.02.25.pdf" style="outline: none;" target="_blank">Styremøte nr. 1

Testregel 2.4.7 (2.4.7 - Nivå AA)
SERIOUS

Element has outline:none which may hide focus indicator
